	function DecreaseSurplassBenefits ()
	{
		window.setTimeout( "TurnOffSurplassBenefits ('surplass_extra')",    500);
/*		window.setTimeout( "TurnOffSurplassBenefits ('surplass_benefits')", 1000); */
		window.setTimeout( "TurnOffSurplassBenefits ('surplass_inday')",    1000); 
	}
		
 	function TurnOffSurplassBenefits (identifier)
	{
		
		if (document.getElementById (identifier + "_title").style.display != "none")
		{
			document.getElementById (identifier + "_title").style.display = "none";
			document.getElementById (identifier + "_gap").style.display = "none";
			document.getElementById (identifier + "_plus").innerHTML = "&nbsp;+";
			
			
			if (identifier == "surplass_inday")
			{
			var vform = document.surplass_inday_page_compare_height;
			var vmany = vform.surplass_inday_min.value;
			}
			
			if (identifier == "surplass_benefits")
			{
			var vform = document.surplass_benefits_page_compare_height;
			var vmany = vform.surplass_benefits_min.value;
			}
			
			if (identifier == "surplass_extra")
			{
			var vform = document.surplass_extra_page_compare_height;
			var vmany = vform.surplass_extra_min.value;
			}
			
			document.getElementById (identifier + "_sty").style.height = vmany;
		}
		else
		{
			document.getElementById (identifier + "_title").style.display = "block";
			document.getElementById (identifier + "_gap").style.display = "block";
			document.getElementById (identifier + "_plus").innerHTML = "&nbsp;^";
			
			if (identifier == "surplass_inday")
			{
			var vform = document.surplass_inday_page_compare_height;
			var vmany = vform.surplass_inday_max.value;
			}
			
			if (identifier == "surplass_benefits")
			{
			var vform = document.surplass_benefits_page_compare_height;
			var vmany = vform.surplass_benefits_max.value;
			}
			
			
			if (identifier == "surplass_extra")
			{
			var vform = document.surplass_extra_page_compare_height;
			var vmany = vform.surplass_extra_max.value;
			}
			
			document.getElementById (identifier + "_sty").style.height = vmany;
			
		}
			
		var form = document.page_compare;
		var many = form.surplass_benefits.value;
		
		var i = 1;

		for(i = 1; i <= many; i++)
		{
		
			if (document.getElementById (identifier + "_" + i).style.display != "none")
			{
				document.getElementById (identifier + "_" + i).style.display = "none";
			}
			else
			{
				document.getElementById (identifier + "_" + i).style.display = "block";
			}
		}
	}
	
	</script><script type="text/javascript" language="JavaScript">	
	var cX = 0;
	var cY = 0;
	var rX = 0;
	var rY = 0;

	function UpdateCursorPosition(e){ cX = e.pageX; cY = e.pageY;}

	function UpdateCursorPositionDocAll(e)
	{
	cX = event.clientX;
	cY = event.clientY;
	}

	if(document.all) { document.onmousemove = UpdateCursorPositionDocAll; }
	else 			 { document.onmousemove = UpdateCursorPosition; }

	function AssignPosition(d,offset)
	{
		if(self.pageYOffset)
		{
			rX = self.pageXOffset;
			rY = self.pageYOffset;
		}
		else if(document.documentElement && document.documentElement.scrollTop)
		{
			rX = document.documentElement.scrollLeft;
			rY = document.documentElement.scrollTop;
		}
		else if(document.body)
		{
			rX = document.body.scrollLeft;
			rY = document.body.scrollTop;
		}

		if(document.all)
		{
			cX += rX;
			cY += rY;
		}

		d.style.left = (cX+30-offset) + "px";
		d.style.top  = (cY+30-70) + "px";
	}

	function HideContent(d)
	{
		if(d.length < 1) { return; }

		document.getElementById(d).style.display = "none";
	}

	function ShowContent(d,offset)
	{
		if(d.length < 1) { return; }

		var dd = document.getElementById(d);
		AssignPosition(dd,offset);
		dd.style.display = "block";

		document.body.appendChild(dd);
	}

	function ReverseContentDisplay(d)
	{
		if(d.length < 1) { return; }

		var dd = document.getElementById(d);
		AssignPosition(dd);
		if(dd.style.display == "none")
		{
			dd.style.display = "block";
		}
		else
		{
			dd.style.display = "none";
		}
	}

	function UpdateSixWeekHighlight(what)
	{	
		var i = 1;

		for(i = 1; i <= 2; i++)
		{
			if (document.getElementById ("policy_sixweek_" + i).checked != true)
			{
			var col = "#dddddd";
			}
			else
			{
			var col = "#A1DE78";
			}
		
			document.getElementById ("sixweek_id_" + i + "_top_curve").style.backgroundColor = col;
			document.getElementById ("sixweek_id_" + i).style.backgroundColor 				= col;
			document.getElementById ("sixweek_id_" + i + "_bot_curve").style.backgroundColor = col;
		}

		if (what > 0)
		{
			if (document.getElementById ("policy_sixweek_" + what).checked != true)
			{
				document.getElementById ("sixweek_id_" + what + "_top_curve").style.backgroundColor = "#D9EFD1";
				document.getElementById ("sixweek_id_" + what).style.backgroundColor 			     = "#D9EFD1";
				document.getElementById ("sixweek_id_" + what + "_bot_curve").style.backgroundColor = "#D9EFD1";
			}
		}
	}
	
	function UpdateSixWeek_Select(what)
	{	
		document.getElementById ("policy_sixweek_" + what).checked = "true";
		
		UpdateSixWeekHighlight(what);
	}

	function UpdateHighlight (what, idname, many)
	{

				var col = "#dddddd";

				var col = "#A1DE78";

		}
	}

	function UpdateHospitalHighlight(what)
	{	
		var form = document.page_hosp;
		
		var many 		= form.howmany.value;
		var maxdisplay 	= form.max_display.value;
			
		var i = 1;

		for(i = 1; i <= many; i++)
		{
			if (document.getElementById ("req_hospital_id_" + i).checked != true)
			{
			var col = "#dddddd";
			}
			else
			{
			var col = "#A1DE78";
			}
		
			document.getElementById ("hospid" + i + "_top_curve").style.backgroundColor = col;
			document.getElementById ("hospid" + i).style.backgroundColor 				= col;
			document.getElementById ("hospid" + i + "_bot_curve").style.backgroundColor = col; if (i-1 < maxdisplay)
				{
				document.getElementById ("hospid" + i + "_top_curve").style.display = "block";
				document.getElementById ("hospid" + i).style.display 				= "block";
				document.getElementById ("hospid" + i + "_bot_curve").style.display = "block";
				document.getElementById ("hospid" + i + "_bot_gap").style.display   = "block";
				}
				else
				{
				document.getElementById ("hospid" + i + "_top_curve").style.display = "none";
				document.getElementById ("hospid" + i).style.display 				= "none";
				document.getElementById ("hospid" + i + "_bot_curve").style.display = "none";
				document.getElementById ("hospid" + i + "_bot_gap").style.display   = "none";
				}}

		if (what > 0)
		{
		if (document.getElementById ("req_hospital_id_" + what).checked != true)
		{
		document.getElementById ("hospid" + what + "_top_curve").style.backgroundColor = "#B1EDB1";
		document.getElementById ("hospid" + what).style.backgroundColor 		  = "#B1EDB1";
		document.getElementById ("hospid" + what + "_bot_curve").style.backgroundColor = "#B1EDB1";
		}
		}
	}
	
	function UpdateHospital_Select(what)
	{	
		document.getElementById ("req_hospital_id_" + what).checked = "true";
		
		UpdateHospitalHighlight(what);
	}
	
	
	function UnHideHospitals()
	{		
		var form = document.page_hosp;   
		
		if (form.max_display.value == 6)
		{ 
			document.getElementById ("max_display").value = "500";
			document.getElementById ("form_button_newgreen").innerHTML  = 'Click Here To Reduce Hospital List';
		}else{
			document.getElementById ("max_display").value = "6";
			document.getElementById ("form_button_newgreen").innerHTML  = 'Click Here To Show More Hospitals';    
		}
		UpdateHospitalHighlight();
	}

	function DisplayMembers()
	{
		var form = document.member_page;
		var many = form.extra_members.selectedIndex+1;

		var i = 1;

		for(i = 1; i < 10; i++)
		{
			document.getElementById ("exmembertr" + i).style.display = "none";
		}

		for (i = 1; i < many; i++)
		{
			document.getElementById ("exmembertr" + i).style.display  = "block";
		}

	
	}

		function numbersonly(evt) 
		{ 
  			var theEvent = evt || window.event; 
  			var key = theEvent.keyCode || theEvent.which; 
  			key = String.fromCharCode( key ); 
  			var regex = /[0-9]|\./; 
  			
  			if( !regex.test(key) ) 
  			{ 
    			theEvent.returnValue = false; 
    			theEvent.preventDefault(); 
  			} 
		}
